This notification is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right to Fair compensation and Transparency in Land acquisition,
Rehabilitation and resettlement Act, 2013 (central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the office of the Collector and Land Acquisition officer on any working day during the working hours
The Government is pleased to authorize the requiring departmet Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department, special project Division,
Tirunelveli and his staff to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper
execution of their work as provided and specified in section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land i.e. sale / purchase, etc
or create any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this notificatrion in the Tamil Nadu Government cazette without prior
approval of the Collector.
objections to the acquisition, if any, may be filed by the person intersted within 60 (sixty) days from the date of publication of this notification in
the Tamil Nadu Government Cazette as provided under section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.

PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
No.ll(2yPwDr348(bS)r2020.
Whereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total ot 120.17.4 hectares
of land is required in Moolakaraipati Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely, Tamirabarani
- Karumeniyar - Nambiyar Interlinking Flood Carrier Canal Project. Environmental lmpact Assessment Study for the irrigation
project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier Canal from Kannadian Channel to Drought prone Areas of Sathankulam and Tisayanvillai
by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar Rivers in Tirunelveli and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamilnadu has been
carried out by "WAPCOS'under the section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the
formation of Flood Carrier Canal . As the Environment lmpact Assessment Study has been carried out for this irrigation
project, Social lmpact Assessment shall not apply according to the provisions of sub section 2 of section 6 of Right to Fair
Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013. The Requisitioning body has
enteredupontheprojectarea on25.02.2019,06.03.2019,20.02.2019,01 .4.2019,02.M.2019and01.08.2019andcanal was
dug to Flood Carrier Project. No family was displaced due to the land acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi is
appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Reseftlement. Therefore, it is notified that for the above said
project in Moolakaraipatti Village of Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District, land measuring an extent of 54.91.91 hectares,
the details of which are specified in the Schedule below, is under acquisition:

acquired to wit for the formation of Ftood carrier canal. As the Environment Impact Assessment study has been carried out for this irrigation project'
social Impact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of sub section 2 of section 6 of Right to Fair compensation and rransparency in
